april 25 , 1993 malaria among u . </s> <s> s . </s> <s> embassy personnel kampala , uganda , 1992 source mmwr 42 15 date apr 23 , 1993 the treatment and prevention of malaria in africa has become a challenging and complex problem because of increasing drug resistance . </s> <s> although the risk of acquiring malaria for u . </s> <s> s . </s> <s> citizens and their dependents stationed overseas generally has been low , this risk varies substantially and unpredictably . </s> <s> during may 1992 , the office of medical services , department of state oms dos , and cdc were notified of an increased number of malaria cases among official u . </s> <s> s . </s> <s> personnel stationed in kampala , uganda . </s> <s> a review of the health records from the embassy health unit ehu in kampala indicated that 27 cases of malaria were diagnosed in official personnel from march through june 1992 compared with two cases during the same period in 1991 . </s> <s> ehu , oms dos , and cdc conducted an investigation to confirm all reported malaria cases and identify potential risk factors for malaria among u . </s> <s> s . </s> <s> embassy personnel . </s> <s> this report summarizes the results of the investigation . </s> <s> malaria blood smears from 25 of the 27 reported case patients were available for review by oms dos and cdc . </s> <s> a case of malaria was confirmed if the slide was positive for plasmodium sp . </s> <s> of the 25 persons , 17 were slide confirmed as having malaria . </s> <s> a questionnaire was distributed to all persons served by the ehu to obtain information about residence , activities , use of malaria chemoprophylaxis , and use of personal protection measures I . </s> <s> e . </s> <s> , using bednets and insect repellents , having window and door screens , and wearing long sleeves and pants in the evening . </s> <s> of the 157 persons eligible for the survey , 128 8 2 responded . </s> <s> risk for malaria was not associated with sex or location of residence in kampala . </s> <s> although the risk for malaria was higher among children aged less than or equal to 15 years 6 32 19 than among persons greater than 15 years 11 94 12 , this difference was not significant relative risk rr 1.6 95 confidence interval ci 0.6 4.0 . </s> <s> eighty two percent of the cases occurred among persons who had been living in kampala for 1 5 years , compared with those living there less than 1 year . </s> <s> travel outside of the kampala area to more rural settings was not associated with increased risk for malaria . </s> <s> four malaria chemoprophylaxis regimens were used by persons who participated in the survey mefloquine , chloroquine and proguanil , chloroquine alone , and proguanil alone . </s> <s> in addition , 23 18 persons who responded were not using any malaria chemoprophylaxis . </s> <s> the risk for malaria was significantly lower among persons using either mefloquine or chloroquine and proguanil 8 8 8 9 than among persons using the other regimens or no prophylaxis 9 37 24 rr 0.4 95 ci 0.2 0.9 . </s> <s> twelve persons not using prophylaxis reported side effects or fear of possible side effects as a reason . </s> <s> the risk for malaria was lower among persons who reported using bednets hicnet medical newsletter page 5 volume 6 , number 11 april 25 , 1993 all or most of the time 2 27 7 than among persons who sometimes or rarely used bednets 15 99 15 rr 0.5 95 ci 0.1 2.0 . </s> <s> the risk for malaria was also lower among persons who consistently used insect repellent in the evening 0 16 , compared with those who rarely used repellent 17 110 15 rr 0 upper 95 confidence limit 1.2 . </s> <s> risk for malaria was not associated with failure to have window or door screens or wear long sleeves or pants in the evening . </s> <s> as a result of this investigation , ehu staff reviewed with all personnel the need to use and comply with the recommended malaria chemoprophylaxis regimens . </s> <s> ehu staff also emphasized the need to use personal protection measures and made plans to obtain insecticide impregnated bednets and to provide window and door screens for all personnel . </s> <s> reported by u . </s> <s> s . </s> <s> embassy health unit , kampala , uganda office of medical svcs , dept of state , washington , d . </s> <s> c . </s> <s> malaria br , div of parasitic diseases , national center for infectious diseases , cdc . </s> <s> editorial note in uganda , the increase in malaria among u . </s> <s> s . </s> <s> personnel was attributed to poor adherence to both recommended malaria chemoprophylaxis regimens and use of personal protection measures during a period of increased malaria transmission and intensified chloroquine resistance in sub saharan africa . </s> <s> the findings in this report underscore the need to provide initial and continued counseling regarding malaria prevention for persons living abroad in malaria endemic areas preventive measures that are also important for short term travelers to such areas . </s> <s> mefloquine is an effective prophylaxis regimen in africa and in most other areas with chloroquine resistant p . </s> <s> falciparum however , in some areas e . </s> <s> g . </s> <s> , thailand , resistance to mefloquine may limit its effectiveness . </s> <s> in africa , the efficacy of mefloquine , compared with chloroquine alone , in preventing infection with p . </s> <s> falciparum is 92 1 . </s> <s> mefloquine is safe and well tolerated when given at 250 mg per week over a 2 year period . </s> <s> the risk for serious adverse reactions possibly associated with mefloquine prophylaxis e . </s> <s> g . </s> <s> , psychosis and convulsions is low I . </s> <s> e . </s> <s> , 1.3 1.9 episodes per 100,000 users 2 , while the risk for less severe adverse reactions e . </s> <s> g . </s> <s> , dizziness , gastrointestinal complaints , and sleep disturbances is similar to that for other antimalarial chemoprophylactics 1 . </s> <s> doxycycline has similar prophylactic efficacy to mefloquine , but the need for daily dosing may reduce compliance with and effectiveness of this regimen 3,4 . </s> <s> chloroquine alone is not effective as prophylaxis in areas of intense chloroquine resistance e . </s> <s> g . </s> <s> , southeast asia and africa . </s> <s> in africa , for persons who cannot take mefloquine or doxycycline , chloroquine and proguanil is an alternative , although less effective , regimen . </s> <s> chloroquine should be used for malaria prevention in areas only where chloroquine resistant p . </s> <s> falciparum has not been reported . </s> <s> country specific recommendations for preventing malaria and information hicnet medical newsletter page 6 volume 6 , number 11 april 11 april 25 , 1993 fda approval of use of a new haemophilus b conjugate vaccine and a combined diphtheria tetanus pertussis and haemophilus b conjugate vaccine for infants and children source mmwr 42 15 date apr 23 , 1993 haemophilus influenzae type b hib conjugate vaccines have been recommended for use in infants since 1990 , and their routine use in infant vaccination has contributed to the substantial decline in the incidence of hib disease in the united states 1 3 . </s> <s> vaccines against diphtheria , tetanus , and pertussis during infancy and childhood have been administered routinely in the united states since the late 1940s and has been associated with a greater than 90 reduction in morbidity and mortality associated with infection by these organisms . </s> <s> because of the increasing number of vaccines now routinely recommended for infants , a high priority is the development of combined vaccines that allow simultaneous administration with fewer separate injections . </s> <s> the food and drug administration fda recently licensed two new products for vaccinating children against these diseases 1 the haemophilus b conjugate vaccine tetanus toxoid conjugate , acthib trademark , for vaccination against hib disease only and 2 a combined diphtheria and tetanus toxoids and whole cell pertussis vaccine dtp and hib conjugate vaccine tetramune trademark , a combination of vaccines formulated for use in vaccinating children against diphtheria , tetanus , pertussis , and hib disease . </s> <s> acthib trademark on march 30 , 1993 , the fda approved a new haemophilus b conjugate vaccine , polyribosylribitol phosphate tetanus toxoid conjugate prp t , manufactured by pasteur merieux serum et vaccins and distributed as acthib trademark by connaught laboratories , inc . </s> <s> swiftwater , pennsylvania . </s> <s> this vaccine has been licensed for use in infants in a three dose primary vaccination series administered at ages 2 , 4 , and 6 months . </s> <s> previously unvaccinated infants 7 11 months of age should receive two doses 2 months apart . </s> <s> previously unvaccinated children 12 14 months of age should receive one dose . </s> <s> a booster dose administered at 15 months of age is recommended for all children . </s> <s> previously unvaccinated children 15 59 months of age should receive a single dose and do not require a booster . </s> <s> more than 90 of infants receiving a primary vaccination series of acthib trademark consecutive doses at 2 , 4 , and 6 months of age develop a geometric mean titer of anti haemophilus b polysaccharide antibody greater than 1 ug ml 4 . </s> <s> this response is similar to that of infants who receive recommended series of previously licensed haemophilus b conjugate vaccines for which efficacy has been demonstrated in prospective trials . </s> <s> two u . </s> <s> s . </s> <s> efficacy trials of prp t were terminated early because of the concomitant licensure of other haemophilus b conjugate vaccines hicnet medical newsletter page 8 volume 6 , number 11 april 25 , 1993 for use in infants 4 . </s> <s> in these studies , no cases of invasive hib disease were detected in approximately 6000 infants vaccinated with prp t . </s> <s> these and other studies suggest that the efficacy of prp t vaccine will be similar to that of the other licensed hib vaccines . </s> <s> tetramune trademark on march 30 , 1993 , the fda approved a combined diphtheria and tetanus toxoids and whole cell pertussis vaccine dtp and haemophilus b conjugate vaccine . </s> <s> tetramune trademark , available from lederle praxis biologicals pearl river , new york , combines two previously licensed products , dtp triimmunol registered , manufactured by lederle laboratories pearl river , new york and haemophilus b conjugate vaccine hibtiter registered , manufactured by praxis biologics , inc . </s> <s> rochester , new york . </s> <s> this vaccine has been licensed for use in children aged 2 months 5 years for protection against diphtheria , tetanus , pertussis , and hib disease when indications for vaccination with dtp vaccine and haemophilus b conjugate vaccine coincide . </s> <s> based on demonstration of co mparable or higher antibody responses to each of the components of the two vaccines , tetramune trademark is expected to provide protection against hib , as well as diphtheria , tetanus , and pertussis , equivalent to that of already licensed formulations of other dtp and haemophilus b vaccines . </s> <s> the advisory committee for immunization practices acip recommends that all infants receive a primary series of one of the licensed haemophilus b conjugate vaccines beginning at 2 months of age and a booster dose at age 12 15 months 5 . </s> <s> the acip also recommends that all infants receive a four dose primary series of diphtheria and tetanus toxoids and pertussis vaccine at 2 , 4 , 6 , and 15 18 months of age , and a booster dose at 4 6 years 6 8 . </s> <s> a complete statement regarding recommendations for use of acthib trademark and tetramune trademark is being developed . </s> <s> reported by office of vaccines research and review , center for biologics evaluation and research , food and drug administration . </s> <s> div of immunization , national center for prevention svcs meningitis and special pathogens br , div of 25 , 1993 dental news international workshop explores oral manifestations of hiv infection nidr research digest written by jody dove march 1993 national institute of dental research at the second international workshop on the oral manifestations of hiv infection , held january 31 february 3 in san francisco , participants explored issues related to the epidemiology , basic molecular virology , mucosal immunology , and oral clinical presentations of hiv infection . </s> <s> the workshop was organized by dr . </s> <s> john greenspan and dr . </s> <s> deborah greenspan of the department of stomatology , school of dentistry , university of california , san francisco . </s> <s> an international steering committee and scientific program committee provided guidance . </s> <s> the conference drew more than 260 scientists from 39 countries , including asia , africa , europe , central america , south america , as well as the united states and canada . </s> <s> support tor the workshop was provided by the national institute of dental research , the national cancer institute , the national institute of allergy and infectious diseases , the nih office of aids research , and the procter and gamble company . </s> <s> among the topics discussed were the epidemiology of hiv lesions ethics , professional responsibility , and public policy occupational issues provision of oral care to the hiv positive population salivary hiv transmission and mucosal immunity opportunistic infections pediatric hiv infection and women s issues . </s> <s> recommendations recommendations emerged from the workshop to define the association between the appearance of oral lesions and rate of progression of hiv , to establish a universal terminology for hiv associated oral lesions , to look for more effective treatments for oral manifestations , to expand molecular biology studies to understand the relationship between hiv infection and common oral lesions , and to study the effects of hiv therapy on oral lesions . </s> <s> epidemiology since the first international workshop on oral manifestations of hiv infection was convened five years ago , the epidemiology of hiv infection has hicnet medical newsletter page 11 volume 6 , number 11 april 25 , 1993 radically changed . </s> <s> in 1988 , hiv infection was detected and reported largely in homosexual and bisexual males , intravenous drug users , and hemophiliacs . </s> <s> today , more hiv infection is seen in heterosexual males and females and in children and adolescents . </s> <s> while the predominant impact of hiv infection has been felt in africa , a major increase in infection rate is being seen in southeast asia as well . </s> <s> five hundred thousand cases have been reported to date in this region and more are appearing all the time . </s> <s> researchers are continuing to document the epidemiology of oral lesions such as hairy leukoplakia and candidiasis . </s> <s> they also are beginning to explore the relationships between specific oral lesions and hiv disease progression and prognosis . </s> <s> social political issues discussion on the social and political implications of hiv infection focused on changing the public s attitude that aids is retribution for indiscriminate sexual behavior and drug use . </s> <s> speakers also addressed health care delivery for hiv infected patients , and the need to educate the public about what aids is , and how it is acquired . </s> <s> saliva and salivary glands conference speakers described transmission issues and the hiv inhibitory activity of saliva , the strength of which varies among the different salivary secretions . </s> <s> whole saliva has a greater inhibitory effect than submandibular secretions , which in turn have a greater inhibitory effect than parotid secretions . </s> <s> research has shown that at least two mechanisms are responsible for salivary inhibitory activity . </s> <s> they attributed the hiv inhibitory effect of saliva to the 1 aggregation agglutination of hiv by saliva , which may both promote clearance of virus and prevent it reaching a target cell , and 2 direct effects on the virus or target cells . </s> <s> other topics discussed were the manifestation of salivary gland disease in hiv infected persons and current research on oral mucosal immunity . </s> <s> pediatric issues pediatric aids recently has emerged as an area of intense interest . </s> <s> with early and accurate diagnosis and proper treatment , the life expectancy of hiv infected children has tripled . </s> <s> the prevention of transmission of hiv from mother to child may be possible in many cases , particularly if the mother s sero status is known prior to giving birth . </s> <s> periodontal and gingival tissue disease hicnet medical newsletter page 12 volume 6 , number 11 april 25 , 1993 oral health researchers continue to explore periodontal diseases and gingivitis found in individuals with hiv infection . </s> <s> recommendations made at the workshop include the standardization of terminology , refinement of diagnostic markers , standardization of study design , and proper consideration of confounding variables resulting from periodontal therapy . </s> <s> occupational and treatment issues occupational issues surrounding the treatment of hiv infected individuals and treatment rendered by hiv infected health care professionals still command considerable attention . </s> <s> factors under consideration include the cost benefit of hiv testing , patient to health care provider transmission of hiv infection and the reverse , and the use of mainstream versus dedicated facilities for the treatment of hiv infected patients . </s> <s> conference participants anticipate that a third international workshop on the oral manifestations of hiv infection will be held in five years or less . </s> <s> proceedings from the second workshop will be published by the quintessence company in late 1993 . </s> <s> end of part 1 internet fax 1 602 451 1165 bitnet atw 1h asuacad fidonet 1 114 15 amateur packet ax25 peter kaminski krillean photography newsgroups m . </s> <s> h . friday , april 30 , at the clinical research meeting . </s>  <s> a press conference will be held at 12 30 p . </s>  <s> m . </s>  <s> gusto evaluates the most aggressive emergency room treatment strategies available to clear blocked heart arteries and restore blood flow to the heart , a process called thrombolysis . </s>  <s> the thrombolytic strategies compared in gusto use powerful drugs to break up blood clots in heart vessels quickly and prevent clots from recurring . </s>  <s> these strategies have never been compared directly in a large scale clinical trial until gusto . </s>  <s> wrote in her previous post in this thread . </s>  <s> in case this puzzles people , I would like to expand on two of her comments . </s>  <s> in article lee lady writes avoiding mistakes is certainly highly desirable . </s>  <s> however it is also widely acknowledged that perfectionism is inimicable to creativity . </s>  <s> ... in the extreme case , a perfectionist becomes so paralyzed by all the possible mistakes he might make that he is unable to even leave the house . </s>  <s> one of the most important and difficult aspects of reasoning about empirical investigation lies in understanding the context , scope , and importance of the various arguments and pieces of evidence that are marshalled for a claim . </s>  <s> some errors break the back of a piece of research , some leave a hole that needs to be filled in , and some are trivial in their importance . </s>  <s> it is a grave mistake to confuse these . </s>  <s> past snippets from this thread I doubt if einstein used any formal methodology . </s>  <s> ... he also proposed numerous experiments which if performed would distinguish a universe in which special relativity holds from one in which it does not . </s>  <s> ... back to lee lady these are not the rules according to many who post to sci.med and sci.psychology . </s>  <s> according to these posters if it s not supported by carefully designed controlled studies then it s not science . </s>  <s> these posters are making the mistake that I have previously criticized of adhering to a methodological recipe . </s>  <s> a carefully designed and controlled study is neither always possible nor always important . </s>  <s> on the other hand , if someone is proposing a remedy that supposedly alleviates a chronic medical problem , we have enough knowledge of the errors that have plagued this kind of claim to ask for a carefully designed and controlled study to alleviate our skepticism . </s>  <s> rules such as support the hypothesis by a carefully designed and controlled study are too narrow to apply to all investigation . </s>  <s> I think that the requirements for particular reasoning to be convincing depends greatly on the kinds of mistakes that have occurred in past reasoning about the same kinds of things . </s>  <s> to reuse the previous example , we know that conclusions from uncontrolled observations of the treatment of chronic medical problems are notoriously problematic . </s>  <s> russell </s>  <s> from gary.schuetter subject a good place for back surgery ? </s>  <s> hello , just one quick question my father has had a back </s>  <s> in article charles l . </s>  <s> creegan writes what about kekule s infamous derivation of the idea of benzene rings from a daydream of snakes in the fire biting their tails ? </s>  <s> is this specific enough to count ? </s>  <s> certainly it turns up repeatedly in basic phil . </s>  <s> of sci . </s>  <s> texts as an example of the inventive component of hypothesizing . </s>  <s> and has been rather thoroughly demolished as myth by robert scott root bernstein . </s>  <s> see his book , discovering . </s>  <s> ring structures for benzene had been proposed before kekule , after him , and at the same time as him . </s>  <s> the current models do not resemble kekule s . </s>  <s> many of the predecessors of kekule s structure resemble the modern model more . </s>  <s> I don t think extra scientific is a very useful phrase in a discussion of the boundaries of science , except as a proposed definiens . </s>  <s> extra rational is a better phrase . </s>  <s> in fact , there are quite a number of well known cases of extra rational considerations driving science in a useful direction . </s>  <s> for example , pasteur discovered that racemic acid was a mixture of enantiomers the origin of stereochemistry partly because he liked a friend s crank theory of chemical action . </s>  <s> the friend was wrong , but pasteur s discovery stood . </s>  <s> a prior investigator mitscherlich , looking at the same phenomenon , had missed a crucial detail presumably because he lacked pasteur s motivation to find something that distinguished racemic acid from tartaric now we say d tartaric acid . </s>  <s> again , pasteur discovered the differential fermentation of enantiomers tartaric acid again not because of some rational conviction , but because he was trying to produce yeast that lived on l tartaric acid . </s>  <s> his notebooks contained fantasies of becoming the newton of mirror image life , which he never admitted publically . </s>  <s> perhaps the best example is the discovery that dna carries genes . </s>  <s> avery started this work because of one of his students , and ardent anglophile and francophobe canadian , defended fred griffiths discoveries in mice . </s>  <s> most of griffiths critics were french , which decided the issue for the student . </s>  <s> avery told him to replicate griffiths work in vitro , which the student eventually did , whereupon avery was convinced and started the research program which , in 15 or so years , produced the famous discovery avery , macleod , and mccarty , jem 1944 . </s>  <s> mark a . burzynski s antineoplastons or information about the current status of his research would be appreciated . </s>  <s> burzynski s work is not too promising . </s>  <s> none of his a 1 through a 5 antineoplastons have been shown to have antineoplastic effects against experimental cancer . </s>  <s> the nci conducted tests of a 2 and a 5 against leukemia in mice , with the result that doses high enough to produce toxic effects in the mice were not effective in inhibiting the growth of the tumor or killing it . </s>  <s> these were in 1983 and 1985 burzynski claims that a 10 is the active factor common to all of a 1 and a 5 something which he has not shown , a 10 has only been extracted from a 2 . </s>  <s> he also hasn t shown that a 1 through a 5 are actually distinct substances . </s>  <s> the nci conducted a series of tests using a 10 against a standard panel of tumors that included different cell lines from tumors in the following classes leukemia , non small cell and small cell lung cancer , colon cancer , cancer of the central nervous system , melanoma , ovarian cancer and renal cancer . </s>  <s> a 10 exhibited neither growth inhibition nor cytotoxicity at the dose levels tested . </s>  <s> it is necessary to process a 10 since it is not soluble burzynski s theory requires soluble agents , but this basically hydrolizes it to pag which he calls as 2.5 . </s>  <s> pag is not an information carrying peptide , something which byrzynski claims is necessary for antineoplastic activity . </s>  <s> as 2.1 also derived from a 10 is a 4 1 mixture of pa and pag . </s>  <s> pa also not a peptide can be purchased at a chemical supply houses for about 0.09 a gram . </s>  <s> a 10 is chemically extremely similar to glutithamide and thalidomide , both of which are habit forming and can cause peripheral neuropathy . </s>  <s> the nasty effects of thalidomide are widely known . </s>  <s> in spite of this similarity , a 10 does not appear to have been tested for it s potential to induce teratogenicity or peripheral neuropathy . </s>  <s> many of burzynski s statements about the origin of his theory , early research , past and present support by others for his work have been shown to be untrue . </s>  <s> sdb </s>  <s> from jim fare subject re endometriosis in article naomi t courter writes can anyone give me more information regarding endometriosis ? </s>  <s> pitt.edu howard r doyle subject re persistent vs chronic in article kxgst1 pitt.edu kenneth gilbert writes in article 1rm29k david rind writes in article horace enea writes can anyone out there tell me the difference between a persistent disease and a chronic one ? </s>  <s> for example , persistent hepatitis vs chronic hepatitis . </s>  <s> I don t think there is a general distinction . </s>  <s> rather , there are two classes of chronic hepatitis chronic active hepatitis and chronic p ersistent hepatitis . </s>  <s> I can t think of any other disease where the term persistent is used with or in preference to chronic . </s>  <s> much as these two terms chronic active and chronic persistent sound fuzzy , the actual distinction between the two conditions is often fairly fuzzy as well . </s>  <s> I beg to differ . </s>  <s> chronic active hepatitis implies that the disease remains active , and generally leads to liver failure . </s>  <s> at the very minimum , the patient has persistently elevated liver enzymes what some call transaminitis . </s>  <s> chronic persistant hepatitis simply means that the patient has hbsag in his her blood and can transmit the infection , but shows no evidence of progressive disease . </s>  <s> if I had to choose , I d much rather have the persistant type . </s>  <s> being a chronic hbsag carrier does not necessarily mean the patient has chronic persistent anything . </s>  <s> persons who are chronic carriers may have no clinical , biochemical , or histologic evidence of liver disease , or they may have chronic persistent hepatitis , chronic active hepatitis , cirrhosis , or hepatocellular carcinoma . </s>  <s> most cases of chronic persistent hepatitis cph are probably the result of a viral infection , although in a good number of cases the cause cannot be determined . </s>  <s> the diagnosis of cph is made on the basis of liver biopsy . </s>  <s> it consists of findings of portal inflammation , an intact periportal limiting plate , and on occasion isolated foci of intralobular necrosis . </s>  <s> but in contrast to chronic active hepatitis cah there is no periportal inflammation , bridging necrosis , or fibrosis . </s>  <s> cph has , indeed , an excellent prognosis . </s>  <s> if I had to choose between cah and cph there is no question I would also choose cph . </s>  <s> however , as david pointed out , the distinction between the two is not as neat as some of us would have it . </s>  <s> the histology can sometimes be pretty equivocal , with biopsies showing areas compatible with both cph and cah . </s>  <s> maybe it is a sampling problem . </s>  <s> maybe it is a continuum . </s>  <s> I don t know . </s>  <s> howard doyle doyle pitt.edu </s>  <s> from james r . </s>  <s> skinner subject re paxil thread a person has crohns , raw vegetables cause problems unspecified steve holland replies patient may have mild obstruction . </s>  <s> avoid things that would plug her up . </s>  <s> crohn s has no dietary restriction in general . </s>  <s> in article , s . </s>  <s> spenser aden wrote interesting statements , simply because I have been told otherwise . </s>  <s> I m certainly not questioning steve s claims , as for one I am not a doctor , and I agree that foods don t bring on the recurrence of crohn s . </s>  <s> but inflammation can be either mildly or drastically enhanced due to food . </s>  <s> the feeling obout this has changed in the gi community . </s>  <s> the current feeling is that inflammation is not induced by food . </s>  <s> there is even evidence that patients deprived of food have mucosal atrophy due to lack of stimulation of intestinal growth factors . </s>  <s> there is now interest in providing small amounts of nasogastric feeding to patients on iv nutrition . </s>  <s> but I digress . </s>  <s> symptoms can be drastically enhanced by food , but not inflammation . </s>  <s> having had one major obstruction resulting in resection is that a good enough caveat , I was told that a low residue diet is called for . </s>  <s> basically , the idea is that if there is inflammation of the gut which may not be realized by the patient , any residue in the system can be caught in the folds of inflammation and constantly irritate , thus exacerbating the problem . </s>  <s> therefore , anything that doesn t digest completely by the point of common inflammation should be avoided . </s>  <s> with what I ve been told is typical crohn s , of the terminal ileum , my diet should be low residue , consisting of completely out never again items o corn kernel husk doesn t digest ... most of us know this o popcorn same o dried dehydrated fruit and fruit skins o nuts very tough when it comes to giving up some fudge the low residue diet is appropriate for you if you still have obstructions . </s>  <s> again , it is not felt that food causes inflammation . </s>  <s> these foods are avoided because they may get stuck . </s>  <s> I d go ahead and have the fudge , though . </s>  <s> discouraged greatly o raw vegetables too fibrous o wheat and raw grain breads o exotic lettuce iceberg is ok since it s apparently mostly water o greens turnip , mustard , kale , etc ... o little seeds , like sesame try getting an arby s without it ! </s>  <s> o long grain and wild rice husky o beans you ll generate enough gas alone without them ! </s>  <s> o basically anything that requires heavy digestive processing I was told that the more processed the food the better ! </s>  <s> rather ironic in this day and age . </s>  <s> the whole point is preventative ... you want to give your system as little chance to inflame as possible . </s>  <s> I was told that among the numerous things that were heavily discouraged I only listed a few , to try the ones I wanted and see how I felt . </s>  <s> if it s bad , don t do it again ! </s>  <s> remember though that this was while I was in remission . </s>  <s> for veggies cook the daylights out of them . </s>  <s> I prefer steaming ... </s>  <s> I think it s cooks more thoroughly you re mileage may vary . </s>  <s> as with anything else , check with your doctor . </s>  <s> don t just take my word . </s>  <s> but this is the info I ve been given , and it may be a starting point for discussion . </s>  <s> good luck ! </s>  <s> spencer makes an especially good point in having an observant and informed patient . </s>  <s> would that many patients be able to tell what causes them problems . </s>  <s> the digestive processing idea is changing , but if a food causes problems , avoid them . </s>  <s> be sure that the foods are tested a second time to be sure the food is a real cause . </s>  <s> crohn s commonly causes intermittent symptoms and some patients end up with severly restricted diets that take months to renormalize . </s>  <s> there was a good article in the ccfa newsletter recently that discussed the issue of dietary restriction of fiber . </s>  <s> it would be worth reading to anyone with an prince writes is there an effect where the doctor believes so strongly in a medicine that he she sees improvement where the is none or sees more improvement than there is ? </s>  <s> if so , what is this effect called ? </s>  <s> is there a reverse of the above effect where the doctor doesn t believe in a medicine and then sees less improvement than there is ? </s>  <s> what would this effect be called ? </s>  <s> have these effects ever been studied ? </s>  <s> how common are these effects ? </s>  <s> thank you in advance for all replies . </s>  <s> these effects are a very real concern in conducting studies of new treatments . </s>  <s> researchers try to limit this kind of effect by performing studies that are blind in various ways . </s>  <s> some of these are o the subjects of the study do not know whether they receive a placebo or the test treatment , I . </s>  <s> e . </s>  <s> , whether they are in the control group or the test group . </s>  <s> o those administering the treatment do not know which subjects receive a placebo or the test treatment . </s>  <s> o those evaluating individual results do not know which subjects receive a placebo or the test treatment . </s>  <s> obviously , at the point at which the data is analyzed , one has to differentiate the test group from the control group . </s>  <s> but the analysis is quasi public the researcher describes it and presents the data on which it is based so that others can verify it . </s>  <s> it is worth noting that in biological studies where the subjects are animals , such as mice , there were many cases of skewed results because those who performed the study did not blind themselves . </s>  <s> it is not considered so important to make mice more ignorant than they already are , though it is important that in all respects except the one tested , the control and test groups are treated alike . </s>  <s> russell </s>  <s> from ron roth subject selective placebo jb ella I baff writes jb jb ron roth is it ? </s>  <s> what causes it ? </s>  <s> could it be caused by a nervous breakdown ? </s>  <s> obesssive compulsive disorder not to be confused with obsessive compulsive personality disorder ! </s>  <s> is an acute anxiety disorder characterized by either obsessions persistent intrusive thoughts that cause anxiety when not entertained , or compulsions repetitive , ritualistic actions that similarly cause intense psychological discomfort when resisted . </s>  <s> ocd is often associated with certain forms of depression . </s>  <s> examples of obsessive thoughts are repeated impulses to kill a loved one though not accompanied by anger , or a religious person having recurrent blasphemous thoughts . </s>  <s> generally , the individual attempts to ignore or suppress the intrusive thoughts by engaging in other activities . </s>  <s> the individual realizes that the thoughts originate from the own mind , rather than being from an external source . </s>  <s> examples of compulsive actions are constant repetitive hand washing , or other activity that is not realistically related to alleviating a source of the anxiety . </s>  <s> in ocd , the obsessions or compulsions are highly distressing to the individual , take an hour or more per day , and significantly impair their daily routine and social relationships . </s>  <s> treatments include psychotherapy , behavioral methods , and sometimes certain anti depressants which have recently been found effective in alleviating obsessions and compulsions . </s>  <s> the standard diagnostic code for ocd , if you want to look it up in the dsm iii manual of psychiatric diagnosis is 300.30 . </s>  <s> kind regards , todd todd I . </s>  <s> stark digital equipment corporation 215 354 1273 philadelphia , pa . </s> methodology in article michael holloway writes in article lee lady writes I would also like to point out that most of the arguments about science in sci.med , sci.psychology , etc . </s>  <s> are not about cases where people are rejecting scientific argument evidence proof . </s>  <s> they are about cases where no adequate scientific research has been done . </s>  <s> in some cases , there is quite a bit of evidence , but it isn t in a format to fit doctrinaire conceptions of what science is . </s>  <s> here it is again . </s>  <s> this indicates confusion between proof and the process of doing science . </s>  <s> you are making precisely one of the points I wanted to make . </s>  <s> I fully agree with you that there is a big distinction between the process of science and the end result . </s>  <s> as an end result of science , one wants to get results that are objectively verifiable . </s>  <s> but there is nothing objective about the process of science . </s>  <s> if good empirical research were done and showed that there is some merit to homeopathic remedies , this would certainly be valuable information . </s>  <s> but it would still not mean that homeopathy qualifies as a science . </s>  <s> this is where you and I disagree with turpin . </s>  <s> in order to have science , one must have a theoretical structure that makes sense , not a mere collection of empirically validated random hypotheses . </s>  <s> experiment and empirical studies are an important part of science , but they are merely the culmination of scientific research . </s>  <s> the most important part of true scientific methodology is scientific thinking . </s>  <s> without this , one does not have any hypotheses worth testing . </s>  <s> no , hypotheses do not just leap out at you after you look at enough data . </s>  <s> nor do they simply come to you in a flash one day while you re shaving or looking out the window . </s>  <s> at least not unless you ve done a lot of really good thinking beforehand . </s>  <s> the difference between a nobel prize level scientist and a mediocre scientist does not lie in the quality of their empirical methodology . </s>  <s> it depends on the quality of their thinking . </s>  <s> it really bothers me that so many graduate students seem to believe that they are doing science merely because they are conducting empirical studies . </s>  <s> and it bothers me even more that there are many fields , such as certain parts of psychology , where there seems to be no thinking at all , but mere studies testing ad hoc hypotheses . </s>  <s> and I m especially offended by russell turpin s repeated assertion that science amounts to nothing more than avoiding mistakes . </s>  <s> simply avoiding mistakes doesn t get you anywhere . </s>  <s> in the arguments between behaviorists and cognitivists , psychology seems less like a science than a collection of competing religious sects . </s>  <s> from sjha cs.cmu.edu somesh jha subject what is requests to the above address , or call 812 471 1990 for more information . </s>  <s> iii . </s>  <s> news from the wires sender jonathan lord subject resurgence of infectious disease concerns cdc date thursday april 15 , 1993 atlanta upi a resurgence of infectious diseases blamed on newly emerging viruses and bacteria pose a major challenge for the nation s health care system , federal health officials said thursday . </s>  <s> the centers for disease control and prevention , reporting its latest findings in an investigation of contaminated hamburger meat that sickened hundreds in 4 states and killed at least four , said it will put renewed emphasis on battling infectious diseases . </s>  <s> part of that emphasis includes a new series titled emerging infectious diseases to be featured in the cdc s morbidity mortality weekly report , which has a wide circulation in the health community . </s>  <s> the issue also will top the agenda of a two day meeting of scientific counselors to update the cdc s draft plan for dealing with the growing threat of infectious ailments . </s>  <s> this is an issue that has been coming and we do have a responsibility to deal with it , said dr . </s>  <s> ruth berkelman , deputy director of the cdc s national center for infectious diseases . </s>  <s> there were more cases of malaria in the u . </s>  <s> s . </s>  <s> in 1992 than in any year since the 1960s , and latin america is experiencing a cholera epidemic , the first in this century , she said . </s>  <s> resistance of disease causing agents to antibiotics is also a problem . </s>  <s> we are seeing much more antibiotic resistance than we have in the past berkleman said . </s>  <s> she said even common ear infections frequently seen in children are becoming resistant to antibiotic treatment . </s>  <s> despite predictions earlier this century that infectious diseases would soon be eliminated as a public health problem , infectious diseases remain the major cause of death worldwide and a leading cause of illness and death in the united states , the cdc said . </s>  <s> it cited the emergence since the 1970s of a myriad of newly identified pathogens and syndromes , such as escherichia coli o157 h7 , a deadly bacterial infection the hepatitis c virus hiv , the virus that causes aids legionnaires disease lyme disease and toxic shock syndrome . </s>  <s> the incidences of many diseases widely presumed to be under control , such as cholera , malaria and tuberculosis , have increased in many areas , the cdc said . </s>  <s> it said efforts at control and prevention have been undermined by drug resistance . </s>  <s> source wall street journal reference 04 15 93 , pb1 headline lyme disease ruling raises liability issues the tick that causes lyme disease may have found a new way to cause damage legal liability . </s>  <s> a federal judge s decision holding a property owner liable for not doing enough to protect workers from lyme disease is getting as much attention as the latest medical study on the disease , a flu like illness that can cause severe physical and mental disabilities and in rare instances death . </s>  <s> the decision last week has put property owners on notice that they may have to do more than protect themselves from the ticks they also may have to protect themselves from litigation if someone becomes infected while on the property . </s>  <s> the decision by u . </s>  <s> s . </s>  <s> district judge robert j . </s>  <s> ward in new york came after a week long trial in a case involving four track workers for the long island railroad . </s>  <s> judge ward found that the workers contracted the disease after they were bitten by ticks while on the job . </s>  <s> he ordered the new york state owned commuter line to pay the workers more than 560,000 to compensate for pain and suffering , in addition to medical expenses and lost wages . </s>  <s> summer camps , schools , companies with facilities in rural or semirural areas , and homeowners who rent to vacationers are among the groups that need to be worried about this ruling , says stephen l . </s>  <s> kass , an attorney at new york law firm berle , kass case , who wrote a legal article three years ago warning property owners of the potential liability . </s>  <s> even a family that invites friends over for a backyard barbecue might be potentially liable . </s>  <s> lawsuits for insect bites , while rare , aren t unheard of . </s>  <s> a summer vacationer in southampton , n . </s>  <s> y . </s>  <s> , last year sued the owner of the home she rented , claiming that a tick on the property gave her rocky mountain spotted fever . </s>  <s> in 1988 , also on long island , a jury ordered an outdoor restaurant to pay more than 3 million to a patron who was stung by a bee , causing an allergic reaction and permanent quadriplegia . </s>  <s> the judge later threw out the award , citing no evidence that a beehive was near the restaurant . </s>  <s> but lawyers say that the attention to lyme disease throughout the country it s most prevalent in new england , the middle atlantic states , wisconsin , minnesota and the northwest may make this particular insect bite a particularly litigious one . </s>  <s> the illness already has proved to be a source of controversy in the courtroom over such issues as the type of medical care insurers will cover and medical malpractice claims against doctors for not diagnosing the disease . </s>  <s> lawyers say worker s compensation claims related to lyme disease have become common in some states in recent years . </s>  <s> payments in worker s compensation cases , however , are limited to medical costs and lost earnings . </s>  <s> the case before judge ward dealt with a potentially much more lucrative avenue for damages , because it involved the question of negligence . </s>  <s> unlike the worker s compensation process , the law governing injuries to rail workers allows for a finding of negligence and , as a result , for additional payments for pain and suffering . </s>  <s> property owners and lawyers say that negligence claims can be made in many other situations where people are exposed to the ticks that carry the disease . </s>  <s> ira m . </s>  <s> maurer , a partner at new york law firm elkind , flynn maurer , who represented the rail workers , says the decision will help to establish the duty of all sorts of property owners to protect against lyme disease . </s>  <s> lawyers caution that despite judge ward s decision , winning a lawsuit for damages caused by lyme disease may prove difficult . </s>  <s> for one thing , victims have to demonstrate that they have pinned down when and where they got the tick bite . </s>  <s> judge ward found that the plaintiffs in the railroad case got lyme disease while working on property owned by the railroad , even though none of the men remembered being bitten . </s>  <s> the workers , who weren t outdoorsmen likely to be exposed elsewhere to the insects , said they saw ticks in the high grass that surrounded some work sites . </s>  <s> a spokeswoman for the railroad says that there was no proof that the four men were bitten while on the job and that the railroad is considering an appeal . </s>  <s> the railroad also disputes judge ward s finding that it didn t do enough to protect employees . </s>  <s> the spokeswoman says the railroad provides track workers with insect repellent and special pants to protect against bug bites . </s>  <s> debate in the scientific community over lyme disease could open up some legal defenses for property owners , such as questioning whether a victim actually has the disease rather than some other illness . </s>  <s> earlier this week , the journal of the american medical association reported that doctors overly diagnose patients as having lyme disease . </s>  <s> and damages awarded to a victim also might be influenced by medical disputes over the degree of harm that lyme disease causes . </s>  <s> because of health and safety concerns , some groups and companies already take special measures to protect against lyme disease . </s>  <s> last year , at its headquarters in franklin lakes , n . </s>  <s> j . </s>  <s> , becton , dickinson co . </s>  <s> began using damminix , a pesticide made by ecohealth inc . </s>  <s> of boston that is designed to kill ticks carrying the disease . </s>  <s> the medical supply company s headquarters include a 120 acre park , and the company was worried that employees who walk on its trails for recreation might get infected . </s>  <s> ruth lister , a spokeswoman for the american camping association in indianapolis , says that many youth camps accredited by her organization also have begun to check children for ticks . </s>  <s> and carole katz , a member of the board of the fire island pines property owners association , says her group spends 30,000 each year to treat their 100 acre site off the coast of new york with the tick killing pesticide . </s>  <s> title urinary dysfunction in lyme disease . </s>  <s> authors chancellor mb mcginnis de shenot pj kiilholma p hirsch ih , department of urology , jefferson medical college , thomas jefferson university , philadelphia , pennsylvania . </s>  <s> reference j urol 1993 jan 149 1 26 30 lyme disease , which is caused by the spirochete borrelia burgdorferi , is associated with a variety of neurological sequelae . </s>  <s> we describe 7 patients with neuro borreliosis who also had lower urinary tract dysfunction . </s>  <s> urodynamic evaluation revealed detrusor hyperreflexia in 5 patients and detrusor areflexia in 2 . </s>  <s> detrusor external sphincter dyssynergia was not noted on electromyography in any patient . </s>  <s> we observed that the urinary tract may be involved in 2 respects in the course of lyme disease 1 voiding dysfunction may be part of neuro borreliosis and 2 the spirochete may directly invade the urinary tract . </s>  <s> in 1 patient bladder infection by the lyme spirochete was documented on biopsy . </s>  <s> neurological and urological symptoms in all patients were slow to resolve and convalescence was protracted . </s>  <s> relapses of active lyme disease and residual neurological deficits were common . </s>  <s> urologists practicing in areas endemic for lyme disease need to be aware of b . </s>  <s> burgdorferi infection in the differential diagnosis of neurogenic bladder dysfunction . </s>  <s> conservative bladder management including clean intermittent catheterization guided by urodynamic evaluation is recommended . </s>  <s> iv . </s>  <s> questions n answers note if you have a response to this question , please forward it to the editor . </s>  <s> sender terry morse what is wrong with the above observation is that it explicitly gives the impression and you may not in fact hold this view that the common perhaps even the correct approach for a scientist to follow is to sit around having flights of fancy and scheming on the basis of his jealousies and petty hatreds . </s>  <s> flights of fancy , and other irrational approaches , are common . </s>  <s> the crucial thing is not to sit around just having fantasies they aren t of any use unless they make you do some experiments . </s>  <s> I ve known a lot of scientists whose fantasies lead them on to creative work usually they won t admit out loud what the fantasy was , prior to the consumption of a few beers . </s>  <s> simple example warren jelinek noticed an extremely heavy band on a dna electrophoresis gel of human alu fragments . </s>  <s> he got very excited , hoping that he d seen some essential part of the control mechanism for eukaryotic genes . </s>  <s> this fantasy led him to sequence samples of the band and carry out binding assays . </s>  <s> the result was a well conserved , 400 or so bp , sequence that occurs about 500,000 times in the human genome . </s>  <s> unfortunately for warren s fantasy , it turns out to be a transposon that is present in so many copies because it replicates itself and copies itself back into the genome . </s>  <s> on the other hand , the characteristics of transposons were much elucidated the necessity of a cellular reverse transcriptase was recognized and the standard method of recognizing human dna was created . </s>  <s> other species have different sets of transposons . </s>  <s> fortunately for me , warren and I used to eat dinner at t . </s>  <s> g . </s>  <s> I . </s>  <s> fridays all the time . </s>  <s> it further at least implicitly advances the position that sciences goes forward and it is not clear what this means given the context in which it occurs by generating in a completely non rational and even random way a plethora of hypotheses and theories that are then weeded out via the critical function of science . </s>  <s> I m not sure that it s random . </s>  <s> but there is no known rational mechanism for generating a rich set of interesting hypotheses . </s>  <s> if you are really working in an unknown area , it is unlikely that you will have much sense of what might or might not be true under those circumstances , the best thing to do is just follow whatever instincts you have . </s>  <s> if they are wrong , you will find out soon enough but at least , you will find out something . </s>  <s> if you try to do experiments at random , with no prior conceptions at all in mind , you will probably get nowhere . </s>  <s> though why this critical function should be less subject to the non rational forces is a mystery . </s>  <s> unfortunately , the critical function does sometimes become hostage to non rational forces . </s>  <s> then we get varieties of pathological science lysenko , mirsky s opposition to dna as gene , cold fusion , and so forth . </s>  <s> if experimental design , hypotheses creation , and theory construction are subject to jealousies and petty hatreds , then this must be equally true of the application of any critical function concerning replication . </s>  <s> this is what leads one ala feyerabend to an anything goes view . </s>  <s> I don t agree that this follows . </s>  <s> in fact , this is exactly the point at which I disagree with feyerabend . </s>  <s> it is a most important part of the culture of science that one keeps one s jealousies out of the refereeing process . </s>  <s> failures there are aplenty , but , on the whole , things work out . </s>  <s> another point there are a couple of senses of the phrase experimental design . </s>  <s> I d say that the less rational part is in experimental choice , not design . </s>  <s> alexander fleming proc . </s>  <s> royal soc . </s>  <s> , 1922 chose to look for bacteriophage in his own mucus for strange reasons phage had previously been found in locust diarrhea fleming probably thought runny bottom , runny nose , what the hell , it s worth a try . </s>  <s> but his method of looking for phage was well designed to detect anything phage like in fact , he found lysozyme . </s>  <s> true , the generation part can be totally irrational . </s>  <s> but typically it is not . </s>  <s> anecdotes concerning instances where a hypothesis seems to have resulted in some way from a dream or from one s political views simply do not generalize well to the actual history of science . </s>  <s> it is not clear to me what you mean by rational vs . </s>  <s> irrational . </s>  <s> perhaps you can give a few examples of surprising experiments that were tried out for perfectly rational reasons , or interesting new theories that were first advanced from logical grounds . </s>  <s> the main examples I can think of are from modern high energy physics which is not typical of science as a whole . </s>  <s> mark a . </s>  <s> fulk university of rochester computer science department </s>  <s> from subject re vasectomy health effects on women ? </s>  <s> in article , eric , a toxicologist who has studied the effects of msg on the brain and on development . </s>  <s> it is undisputed in the literature that msg is an excitotoxic food additive , and that its major commencing in june 1993 and january 1994 . </s>  <s> program objectives the program intends to promote technology transfer between japan and the united states . </s>  <s> it is also designed to let scientists , engineers , and managers experience how the japanese proceed with technological development . </s>  <s> this is facilitated by extended internships in japanese research facilities and laboratories that provide participants with the opportunity to develop long term professional relationships with their japanese counterparts . </s>  <s> program design to fulfill the objectives of the program , participants will be required to develop advanced language capability and a deep understanding of japan and its culture . </s>  <s> correspondingly , jstmp consists of three major components 1 . </s>  <s> training in the japanese language several japanese language courses will be offered , including intensive courses designed to expedite language preparation for scientists and engineers in a relatively short time . </s>  <s> 2 . </s>  <s> education in japanese business and social culture a particular enphasis is placed on attaining a deep understanding of the cultural and educational basis of japanese management approaches in manufacturing and information technology . </s>  <s> courses will be available in a variety of departments throughout both universities including anthropology , sociology , history , and political science . </s>  <s> moreover , seminars and colloquiums will be conducted . </s>  <s> further , a field trip to japanese manufacturing or research facilities in the united states will be scheduled . </s>  <s> 3 . </s>  <s> an internship or a study mission in japan upon completion of their language and cultural training at pitt and cmu , participants will have the opportunity to go to japan and observe , and participate in the management of technology . </s>  <s> internships in japan will generally run for one year however , shorter ones are possible . </s>  <s> fellowships covering tuition for language and culture courses , as well as stipends for living expenses are available . </s>  <s> for more information and application understand it the following is based on copies I was given of some articles published in hearing instruments . </s>  <s> I would appreciate any comments about this and other new technology for hearing aids . </s>  <s> the resound system was developed on the basis of some research at at t and appears to take a different approach from other aids . </s>  <s> it appears to me that a new programmable aid like the widex just uses a more flexible and programmable version of the classical approach of amplifying some parts of the spectrum more than others and adding some compression to try and help out in noisy situations . </s>  <s> the major difference in the resound approach is that it divides the spectrum into low and high frequencies splitting point is programmable , apparently based on the fact that lots of vowel information can be found in the low frequencies , while the important consonant information unfortunately for me is in the high frequencies . </s>  <s> the two bands then are treated with different compression schemes which are programable . </s>  <s> they have also developed a new fitting algorythm that builds on what they call abnormal growth of loudness . </s>  <s> this latter is interesting and fits my own personal experience , though I think the phrase is missleading . </s>  <s> what appears to be the case is that as you exceed the minimum threshold for a person with hearing loss , the deficit becomes progresslively less compared to normals and by the time you reach the too loud point the sensitivity curves appear to converge . </s>  <s> this means that if you just boost all sound levels , you are overloading at the high end for people with hearing losses . </s>  <s> hence what you want is progressively less amplification as the signal get closer to the maximum tolerable point . </s>  <s> you want to boost low volume sounds more than high and do so potentially differently for the low and high frequency parts of the spectrum specially for someone like me who is relatively normal up to 1000 cps and then falls off a cliff . </s>  <s> aids with simple compressors don t descriminate between energy in the low and high frequencies and can therefor compress useful high frequency information because of high volume of low frequency components . </s>  <s> particularly impressive was the resound performance with whispered speech and in simulated restaurant noise situations . </s>  <s> rich haller university of oregon , eugene , or , usa </s>  <s> from subject lupus I have a friend who has just been diagnosed with lupus , and I know nothing </s>  <s> it is used to form glucose tolerance factor gtf . </s>  <s> gtf is made up of chromium , nicinamide niacin , glycine , cysteine and glutamic . </s>  <s> only the chromium and the niacin are needed from the diet to form gtf . </s>  <s> some foods already have gtf liver , brewers or nutritional yeast , and black pepper . </s>  <s> when chromium is in gtf , a pretty good absorption is seen about 20 . </s>  <s> but when it is simply present as a mineral or mineral chelate chromium picolinate it s absorption is much lower 1 to 2 , lowest for all the minerals . </s>  <s> I ve been posting bioavailability . </s>  <s> when yeast gtf is used , good results are obtained but when chromium itself is used the results are usually negative . </s>  <s> in addition to type ii diabetes , chromiuum metabolic function . </s>  <s> if this eye focusing activity is impaired by a lack of glucose due to a poor insulin response , intraocular pressure is believed to be elevated . </s>  <s> in a fairly homeopathy ... tradition ? </s>  <s> in article , mark fulk writes 2 science has not historically progressed in any sort of rational experiment data theory sequence . </s>  <s> most experiments are carried out , and interpreted , in pre existing theoretical frameworks . </s>  <s> the theoretical controversies of the day determine which experiments get done . </s>  <s> overall , there is a huge messy affair of personal jealousies , crazy motivations , petty hatreds , and the like that determines which experiments , and which computations , get done . </s>  <s> what keeps it going forward is the critical function of science results don t count unless they can be replicated . </s>  <s> the whole system is a sort of mechanism for generate and test . </s>  <s> the generate part can be clear what this means given the context in which it occurs by generating in a completely non rational and even random way a plethora of hypotheses and theories that are then weeded out via the critical function of science . </s>  <s> though why this critical function should be less subject to the non rational forces is a mystery . </s>  <s> if experimental design , hypotheses creation , and radioactive tracer , and an imaging device is used to track the distribution of the tracer wwithin the body . </s>  <s> the tracer is usually given intravenously . </s>  <s> iv this means that the physician or his assistant will insert a needle into a vein and inject medicine into the vein . </s>  <s> after a few minutes has passed for the tracer to circulate through the body , the person is scanned with an imaging device to detect high concentrations of the tracer . </s>  <s> the radiologist or doctor is looking for areas that take up more of the radioactive tracer or less of it . </s> be turned into an ad hoc rsi management tool . </s>  <s> or , any batch queue submission program that lets you submit a program to run at a specific time to display a message to the screen . </s>  <s> using windows as an example create a calendar file , and include this filename in your win.ini s load line so you get it on every startup of windows . </s>  <s> suppose you want to have breaks every 30 minutes , starting from 9 am . </s>  <s> press f7 special time ... to enter an appointment , enter 9 30 , hit enter , and type some text in saying what the break is for . </s>  <s> then press f5 to </s>  <s> put this file on your run line , as above , and you will then , with a single keypress , be able to set up your daily appointments with rsi exercises . </s>  <s> the above method should be
